Summary of the hot and cold lines in XMon

* A script looks at XMon hot and cold trigger lines every 20 minutes.
  This file is the summary of what it finds.

* First line is run number, number of entries, and the physics table.

* Additional lines are listed in order of problems
  * xx% is percentage of time this line is either hot or cold
  * how many times hot/cold is listed after the trigger name

* Problems that have both hot and cold entries are probably a result
  of the allowed range being set too small.

Last updated: Mon May 12 11:58:30 CDT 2003
